### NI VeriStand .NET API Reference

This API reference provides information about the programmatic elements available for this product.

#### Looking for Something Else?

For information not found in the API Reference for your product, such as detailed descriptions of the product functionality and the step by step processes for use, browse *Related Information*.

Related information:

- Software and Driver Downloads
- Release Notes

### AcknowledgementStatus Enumeration

Specifies the acknowledgement status of an alarm.

#### Syntax

**Namespace:**[NationalInstruments.VeriStand.ClientAPI](nationalinstruments-veristand-clientapi.html)

public enum AcknowledgementStatus

#### Members

| Name | Value | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Unacknowledged | 0 | Specifies the alarm is unacknowledged. |
| Acknowledged | 1 | Specifies the alarm is acknowledged. |

### AlarmChangeEventArgs Class

Provides data about an alarm event.

#### Derives from

- EventArgs

#### Syntax

**Namespace:**[NationalInstruments.VeriStand.ClientAPI](nationalinstruments-veristand-clientapi.html)

public class AlarmChangeEventArgs : EventArgs

#### Properties

| Name | Description |
| --- | --- |
| AcknowledgeFlag | Gets the data for the acknowledge flag. |
| AlarmInfo | Gets the AlarmInfo of the alarm. |
| AlarmName | Gets the name of the alarm. |
| ClearedFlag | Gets the data for the cleared flag. |
| Flag | Gets the alarm flag type. |
| Path | Gets the path to the alarm. |
| SetFlag | Gets the data for the set flag. |
| Target | Gets the target of the alarm. |
| Value | Gets the value of the alarm. |

## TOPIC 00028: HighLimitIsConstant

- bundle_id: `veristand-net-api-ref`
- source_path: `nationalinstruments-veristand-clientapi-alarminfo-highlimitisconstant.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/veristand-net-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/nationalinstruments-veristand-clientapi-alarminfo-highlimitisconstant.html
- document_id: `veristand-net-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Indicates whether the value to use for the high limit is a constant value or the value of a channel in the system. If TRUE, the high limit is the value specified by HighLimit. If FALSE, the high limit is the value of the channel specified by HighLimitChannelName. SyntaxNamespace: NationalInstruments

### HighLimitIsConstant

Indicates whether the value to use for the high limit is a constant value or the value of a channel in the system. If TRUE, the high limit is the value specified by [HighLimit](nationalinstruments-veristand-clientapi-alarminfo-highlimit.html). If FALSE, the high limit is the value of the channel specified by [HighLimitChannelName](nationalinstruments-veristand-clientapi-alarminfo-highlimitchannelname.html).

#### Syntax

**Namespace:**[NationalInstruments.VeriStand.ClientAPI](nationalinstruments-veristand-clientapi.html)

public bool HighLimitIsConstant

Parent topic:

AlarmInfo Class

- source_path: `nationalinstruments-veristand-clientapi-alarminfo-priority.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/veristand-net-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/nationalinstruments-veristand-clientapi-alarminfo-priority.html
- document_id: `veristand-net-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: This property is deprecated in NI VeriStand 2011 and later. Use the PriorityNumber property instead. SyntaxNamespace: NationalInstruments.VeriStand.ClientAPIpublic AlarmPriority Priority { get; set; }RemarksGets or sets the priority of an alarm running on the target.Setting this property to Low, Med

### Priority

This property is deprecated in NI VeriStand 2011 and later. Use the [PriorityNumber](nationalinstruments-veristand-clientapi-alarminfo-prioritynumber.html) property instead.

#### Syntax

**Namespace:**[NationalInstruments.VeriStand.ClientAPI](nationalinstruments-veristand-clientapi.html)

public [AlarmPriority](nationalinstruments-veristand-clientapi-alarmpriority.html) Priority { get; set; }

#### Remarks

Gets or sets the priority of an alarm running on the target.

Setting this property to Low, Medium, or High automatically sets the [PriorityNumber](nationalinstruments-veristand-clientapi-alarminfo-prioritynumber.html) to 25, 15, or 5, respectively.

Parent topic:

AlarmInfo Class

### AlarmInfo Class

| --- | --- |

| ClearedFlag | Data for cleared flag of the alarm. |
| DelayDuration | The amount of time the WatchChannel value must be outside the alarm limits before the alarm is triggered. |
| FullName | The path to the alarm relative to the alarms section. |
| GroupNumber | The number of the group to which the alarm belongs. |
| HighLimit | The value to use for the high limit of the acceptable range if HighLimitIsConstant is TRUE. If the value of WatchChannel exceeds this limit, the alarm is triggered. |

| LowLimitIsConstant | Indicates whether the value to use for the low limit is a constant value or the value of a channel in the system. If TRUE, the low limit is the value specified by LowLimit. If FALSE, the low limit is the value of the channel specified by LowLimitChannelName. |

| Name | The name of the alarm. |
| ProcedureName | The name of the procedure to initiate when the alarm occurs. |
| SetFlag | Data for set flag of the alarm. |
| State | The AlarmState. |
| TripValue | The value at which the alarm was last triggered. |

## TOPIC 00042: AlarmMode Enumeration

- bundle_id: `veristand-net-api-ref`
- source_path: `nationalinstruments-veristand-clientapi-alarmmode.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/veristand-net-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/nationalinstruments-veristand-clientapi-alarmmode.html
- document_id: `veristand-net-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: The operating mode of an alarm running on the target. The operating mode of an alarm specifies the action that occurs when the alarm is triggered. SyntaxNamespace: NationalInstruments.VeriStand.ClientAPIpublic enum AlarmModeMembersNameValueDescriptionNormal0The alarm trips if the WatchChannel is out

### AlarmMode Enumeration

The operating mode of an alarm running on the target. The operating mode of an alarm specifies the action that occurs when the alarm is triggered.

#### Syntax

**Namespace:**[NationalInstruments.VeriStand.ClientAPI](nationalinstruments-veristand-clientapi.html)

public enum AlarmMode

#### Members

| Name | Value | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Normal | 0 | The alarm trips if the WatchChannel is outside the high or low limits. |
| IndicateOnly | 1 | The alarm only monitors the WatchChannel value. If the channel value is outside the high or low limits, AlarmState returns Indicate. No procedure executes in response to the alarm. |

Parent topic:

NationalInstruments.VeriStand.ClientAPI

<!--NI_TOPIC bundle=veristand-net-api-ref path=nationalinstruments-veristand-clientapi-alarmpriority.html language=enus -->

| Name | Value | Description |

| Low | 0 | The alarm is low-priority. |
| Medium | 1 | The alarm is medium-priority. |
| High | 2 | The alarm is high-priority. |

Parent topic:

## TOPIC 00044: AlarmState Enumeration

- bundle_id: `veristand-net-api-ref`
- source_path: `nationalinstruments-veristand-clientapi-alarmstate.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/veristand-net-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/nationalinstruments-veristand-clientapi-alarmstate.html
- document_id: `veristand-net-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: The state of an alarm running on the target. SyntaxNamespace: NationalInstruments.VeriStand.ClientAPIpublic enum AlarmStateMembersNameValueDescriptionDisabled0The alarm is inactive. The alarm does not trip even if the WatchChannel value is outside the limits. Enabled1The alarm is active. The alarm t

### AlarmState Enumeration

The state of an alarm running on the target.

#### Syntax

**Namespace:**[NationalInstruments.VeriStand.ClientAPI](nationalinstruments-veristand-clientapi.html)

public enum AlarmState

#### Members

| Name | Value | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Disabled | 0 | The alarm is inactive. The alarm does not trip even if the WatchChannel value is outside the limits. |
| Enabled | 1 | The alarm is active. The alarm trips if the WatchChannel value is outside the limits. |
| Tripped | 2 | The alarm tripped and the procedure associated with the alarm was initiated. |
| DelayedTripped | 3 | The WatchChannel value is outside the limits, but the alarm has not tripped because the DelayDuration time has not elapsed. If the DelayDuration elapses and WatchChannel remains outside the limits, the alarm state changes to Tripped or Indicate, depending on the AlarmMode. |
| Indicate | 4 | The WatchChannel value is outside the limits, but the alarm was not tripped because AlarmMode is IndicateOnly. |

Parent topic:

## TOPIC 00050: AlarmStateWatcher Class

- bundle_id: `veristand-net-api-ref`
- source_path: `nationalinstruments-veristand-clientapi-alarmstatewatcher.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/veristand-net-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/nationalinstruments-veristand-clientapi-alarmstatewatcher.html
- document_id: `veristand-net-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: This class essentially serves as a wrapper around the alarm state change event (specific to one alarm) for the purpose of allowing access to this event easier to obtain from within LabVIEW. Constructing and destructing the object registers and unregisters, respectively, from the event. Then, LabVIEW

### AlarmStateWatcher Class

This class essentially serves as a wrapper around the alarm state change event (specific to one alarm) for the purpose of allowing access to this event easier to obtain from within LabVIEW. Constructing and destructing the object registers and unregisters, respectively, from the event. Then, LabVIEW users can register to the event within this class for use in the event structure in LabVIEW.

#### Derives from

- IDisposable

#### Syntax

**Namespace:**[NationalInstruments.VeriStand.ClientAPI](nationalinstruments-veristand-clientapi.html)

public class AlarmStateWatcher : IDisposable

#### Constructors

| Name | Description |
| --- | --- |
| AlarmStateWatcher(IAlarmManager2, string, string) | Initializes a new instance of the AlarmStateWatcher class. |

#### Methods

| Name | Description |
| --- | --- |
| Dispose() | Explicit disposal method. |
| Dispose(bool) | Dispose method according to the IDisposable design pattern. |
| OnAlarmStateChange(object, AlarmChangeEventArgs) | Method used to interface between the event in the IAlarmManager2 and the event in the AlarmStateWatcher class. |

#### Events

| Name | Description |
| --- | --- |
| AlarmStateChangeEventHandler | Event to register a callback to receive notifications when alarm state changes. |

Parent topic:

| Coefficients | Gets a value indicating the coefficients that define the polynomial equation used to calibrate the channel. |
| Remove | Gets a value indicating whether to remove the calibration from the channel. |

## TOPIC 00072: ChannelValueWatcher Class

- bundle_id: `veristand-net-api-ref`
- source_path: `nationalinstruments-veristand-clientapi-channelvaluewatcher.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/veristand-net-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/nationalinstruments-veristand-clientapi-channelvaluewatcher.html
- document_id: `veristand-net-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: This class essentially serves as a wrapper around the channel value change event (specific to one parameter) for the purpose of allowing access to this event easier to obtain from within LabVIEW. Constructing and destructing the object registers and unregisters, respectively, from the event. Then, L

### ChannelValueWatcher Class

This class essentially serves as a wrapper around the channel value change event (specific to one parameter) for the purpose of allowing access to this event easier to obtain from within LabVIEW. Constructing and destructing the object registers and unregisters, respectively, from the event. Then, LabVIEW users can register to the event within this class for use in the event structure in LabVIEW.

#### Derives from

- IDisposable

#### Syntax

**Namespace:**[NationalInstruments.VeriStand.ClientAPI](nationalinstruments-veristand-clientapi.html)

public class ChannelValueWatcher : IDisposable

#### Constructors

| Name | Description |
| --- | --- |
| ChannelValueWatcher(IChannelMonitor, string) | Initializes a new instance of the ChannelValueWatcher class. |

#### Methods

| Name | Description |
| --- | --- |
| Dispose() | Explicit disposal method. |
| Dispose(bool) | Dispose method according to the IDisposable design pattern. |
| OnChannelValueChange(object, ChannelValueChangeEventArgs) | Method used to interface between the event in the IChannelMonitor and the event in the ChannelValueWatcher class. |

#### Events

| Name | Description |
| --- | --- |
| ChannelValueChangeEventHandler | Event to register a callback to receive notifications when channel values are changed. |

Parent topic:

SyntaxNamespace: NationalInstruments.VeriStand.ClientAPIpublic IProject GetIP

### GetIProject(string, string, string, string, out Error)

Gets the [IProject](nationalinstruments-veristand-clientapi-iproject.html) interface, which you can use to interact with an NI VeriStand project. You can open, deploy, run, close, and undeploy the project, open the Workspace window or a tool, and send messages to specific tools.

#### Syntax

**Namespace:**[NationalInstruments.VeriStand.ClientAPI](nationalinstruments-veristand-clientapi.html)

public [IProject](nationalinstruments-veristand-clientapi-iproject.html) GetIProject(string gateway_ip_address, string project_path, string username, string password, out Error error)

#### Parameters

| Name | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| gateway_ip_address | string | Specifies the IP address of the VeriStand Gateway |
| project_path | string | Specifies the path to the NI VeriStand project with which to interact. |
| username | string | Specifies the user name to use to access the NI VeriStand project. |
| password | string | Specifies the password associated with the username you enter. |
| error | out Error | Indicates any error that occurs while opening the project. |

#### Returns

Returns an [IProject](nationalinstruments-veristand-clientapi-iproject.html) object.

Parent topic:

Factory Class

- page_type: `leaf`

- source_description: Constant that can be used for all requests to the localhost. SyntaxNamespace: NationalInstruments.VeriStand.ClientAPIpublic const string LocalIpAddr

### LocalIpAddress

public const string LocalIpAddress

## TOPIC 00133: StartGatewayAndProjectServerAsync(ServerCreateOptions)

- bundle_id: `veristand-net-api-ref`
- source_path: `nationalinstruments-veristand-clientapi-factory-startgatewayandprojectserverasync__servercreateoptions.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/veristand-net-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/nationalinstruments-veristand-clientapi-factory-startgatewayandprojectserverasync__servercreateoptions.html
- document_id: `veristand-net-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Start up the Gateway via the VeriStand Project Explorer on the localhost. This is necessary if you intend to use IProject. SyntaxNamespace: NationalInstruments.VeriStand.ClientAPIpublic Task StartGatewayAndProjectServerAsync(ServerCreateOptions options)RemarksWill throw TimeoutException if the serve

### StartGatewayAndProjectServerAsync(ServerCreateOptions)

Start up the Gateway via the VeriStand Project Explorer on the localhost. This is necessary if you intend to use [IProject](nationalinstruments-veristand-clientapi-iproject.html).

#### Syntax

**Namespace:**[NationalInstruments.VeriStand.ClientAPI](nationalinstruments-veristand-clientapi.html)

public Task StartGatewayAndProjectServerAsync(ServerCreateOptions options)

#### Remarks

Will throw TimeoutException if the server process does not start in time, or various file exceptions if it fails to run the server process executable.

#### Parameters

| Name | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| options | ServerCreateOptions | Server creation options |

#### Returns

Task that can be awaited. After completion, getting any of the other interfaces should be possible.

Parent topic:

### Factory Class

Provides access to the NI VeriStand system and the various interfaces available in the Execution API. Any code you write using this API must include a Factory constructor to access NI VeriStand.

#### Derives from

None

#### Syntax

**Namespace:**[NationalInstruments.VeriStand.ClientAPI](nationalinstruments-veristand-clientapi.html)

public class Factory

#### Remarks

For example code and more information about accessing this class, refer to one of the following help topics:

LabVIEW Walkthrough: Opening and Running a Project

C# Walkthrough: Opening and Running a Project

#### Constructors

| Name | Description |
| --- | --- |
| Factory() | Constructor for Factory. |

#### Fields

| Name | Description |
| --- | --- |
| LocalIpAddress | Constant that can be used for all requests to the localhost. Note, string.empty and localhost are not exactly the same, and may behave slightly differently based on what ethernet adapters exist on a given system. |

#### Methods

| Name | Description |
| --- | --- |
| GetActiveProjects(string) | Returns a list of paths to currently open NI VeriStand projects. |
| GetActiveProjects(string, out Error) | Returns a list of paths to currently open NI VeriStand projects. If an error occurs, this instance outputs an error object. |
| GetAllDeployedSessions(string, out Error) | Gets a list of session IDs for all currently deployed sessions. If an error occurs, this instance outputs an error object. |
| GetAllDeployedSessions(string) | Gets a list of session IDs for all currently deployed sessions. |
| GetChannelMonitor() | Gets the IChannelMonitor interface, which you can use to register and deregister for Channel Value Change Events. |
| GetChannelMonitor(string) | Gets the IChannelMonitor interface, which you can use to register and deregister for Channel Value Change Events. |
| GetIAlarm(string, string, string) | Gets the IAlarm interface, which you can use to get and set data for a single alarm, enable or disable the alarm, and set the alarm mode. |
| GetIAlarm(string) | This method is deprecated in NI VeriStand 2010 and later. Use the GetIAlarm(string) method instead. |
| GetIAlarmManager() | This method is deprecated in NI VeriStand 2010 and later. Use the GetIAlarmManager2 method instead. |
| GetIAlarmManager2(string) | Gets the IAlarmManager2 interface, which you can use to get a list of alarms configured on the system and the status of those alarms. |
| GetICalibration(string) | Gets the ICalibration interface, which you can use to get and set the calibration settings of scalable channels. |
| GetICalibration2(string) | Gets the ICalibration2 interface, which you can use to get and set the calibration settings of scalable channels. |
| GetIChannelFault(string) | Gets the IChannelFault interface, which you can use to view, set, and clear channel software faults on the execution host. |
| GetIChannelFault() | This method is deprecated in NI VeriStand 2010 and later. Use the GetIChannelFault(string) method instead. |
| GetICustomDevice(string, string) | Gets the ICustomDevice interface, which you can use to send messages to a custom device. |
| GetIDataLogging(string) | Gets the IDataLogging interface, which you can use to automate data logging in the VeriStand Gateway. |
| GetIDiagnostics(string) | Gets the IDiagnostics interface, which can be used to enable, disable, and check the status of Perfetto on the VeriStand engine. |
| GetIErrorProviding(string) | Gets the IErrorProviding interface, which you can use to translate electrical errors into channel value pairs. |
| GetIErrorProviding() | Gets the IErrorProviding interface, which you can use to translate electrical errors into channel value pairs. |
| GetIMacroPlayer(string) | Gets the IMacroPlayer interface, which you can use to interact with the Macro Player tool. Use this interface to load a macro (.nivsmacro) file you created using the IMacroRecorder interface or the Macro Recorder tool in NI VeriStand, and to play back the commands NI VeriStand sent to the execution host during the time the Macro Recorder ran. |
| GetIMacroRecorder() | Gets the IMacroRecorder interface, which you can use to interact with the Macro Recorder tool. Use this interface to record the commands NI VeriStand sends to an RT target or desktop PC, and to create a macro (.nivsmacro) file you can play back using the methods of the IMacroPlayer interface. |
| GetIModel(string, string, string) | Gets the IModel interface, which you can use to get information about and configure the execution state of a single model. |
| GetIModel(string) | This method is deprecated in NI VeriStand 2010 and later. Use the GetIModel(string) method instead. |
| GetIModelManager() | This method is deprecated in NI VeriStand 2010 and later. Use the GetIModelManager2 method instead. |
| GetIModelManager2(string) | Gets the IModelManager2 interface, which you can use to get lists of the models and model parameters in the system and to get and set the values of model parameters. |
| GetIProject(string, string, string, string) | Gets the IProject interface, which you can use to interact with an NI VeriStand project. You can open, deploy, run, close, and undeploy the project, open the Workspace window or a tool, and send messages to specific tools. |
| GetIProject(string, string, string, string, out Error) | Gets the IProject interface, which you can use to interact with an NI VeriStand project. You can open, deploy, run, close, and undeploy the project, open the Workspace window or a tool, and send messages to specific tools. |
| GetIRuntimeConfigurationManager(string) | Gets the IRuntimeConfigurationManager interface, which you can use to apply or remove runtime configurations from the custom device. |
| GetIStimulus() | This method is deprecated in NI VeriStand 2010 and later. Use the GetIStimulusProfileSession method instead. |
| GetIStimulus2(string) | This method is deprecated in NI VeriStand 2011 and later. Use the GetIStimulusProfileSession method instead. Gets the IStimulus2 interface, which you can use to access the stimulus profile, get information about stimulus generation, and run and stop stimulus generation. |

| GetIWorkspace2() | Gets the IWorkspace2 interface, which you can use to manage connections between the VeriStand Gateway and one or more targets, to start and stop data logging operations, and to configure events for error and status notifications. This method assumes that the VeriStand Gateway is running on the localhost. |
| GetIWorkspace2(string) | Gets the IWorkspace2 interface, which you can use to manage connections between the VeriStand Gateway and one or more targets, to start and stop data logging operations, and to configure events for error and status notifications. This method allows you to specify the IP address of the VeriStand Gateway. |

| StartGatewayAndProjectServerAsync() |  |

### GetAlarmData(out AlarmInfo, uint)

Accesses information about an alarm.

#### Syntax

**Namespace:**[NationalInstruments.VeriStand.ClientAPI](nationalinstruments-veristand-clientapi.html)

- content_type: `reference`

SyntaxNamespace: NationalInstruments.VeriStand.ClientAPIpublic Error GetAlarmsStatus(

### GetAlarmsStatus(out bool, out bool, out bool, out string, out string, out string)

This method is obsolete in NI VeriStand 2011 and later. Use the [GetMultipleAlarmsData](nationalinstruments-veristand-clientapi-ialarmmanager2-getmultiplealarmsdata__string-string_arr1-uint-out.html) method of the [IAlarmManager2](nationalinstruments-veristand-clientapi-ialarmmanager2.html) interface instead, which allows you to get specific information about an alarm, such as its status.

#### Syntax

**Namespace:**[NationalInstruments.VeriStand.ClientAPI](nationalinstruments-veristand-clientapi.html)

public [Error](nationalinstruments-veristand-clientapi-stimulusresult.html) GetAlarmsStatus(out bool highAlarm, out bool medAlarm, out bool lowAlarm, out string highAlarmName, out string medAlarmName, out string lowAlarmName)

#### Remarks

Strict priorities of low, medium, and high are no longer supported. Valid priorities now range from 0 - 31. This method only tests alarms in group 0.

#### Parameters

| Name | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| highAlarm | out bool | Returns TRUE if a high-priority alarm is triggered. |
| medAlarm | out bool | Returns TRUE if a medium-priority alarm is triggered. |
| lowAlarm | out bool | Returns TRUE if a low-priority alarm is triggered. |
| highAlarmName | out string | Returns the name of the currently active, high-priority alarm. |
| medAlarmName | out string | Returns the name of the currently active, medium-priority alarm. |
| lowAlarmName | out string | Returns the name of the currently active, low-priority alarm. |

#### Returns

Returns an NationalInstruments.VeriStand.Error object. If no error occurs, the Code property of the Error object is 0.

Parent topic:

IAlarmManager Interface

### GetMultipleAlarmsData(string[], uint, out AlarmInfo[])

This method from the IAlarmManager interface gets a list of all the alarms running on the first target. However, National Instruments recommends that you use the [GetMultipleAlarmsData](nationalinstruments-veristand-clientapi-ialarmmanager2-getmultiplealarmsdata__string-string_arr1-uint-out.html) method of the [IAlarmManager2](nationalinstruments-veristand-clientapi-ialarmmanager2.html) interface instead of this deprecated method.

#### Syntax

**Namespace:**[NationalInstruments.VeriStand.ClientAPI](nationalinstruments-veristand-clientapi.html)

public [Error](nationalinstruments-veristand-clientapi-stimulusresult.html) GetMultipleAlarmsData(string[] alarmNames, uint timeout, out AlarmInfo[] alarmInfo)

#### Remarks

You must use the [GetMultipleAlarmsData](nationalinstruments-veristand-clientapi-ialarmmanager2-getmultiplealarmsdata__string-string_arr1-uint-out.html) method of the [IAlarmManager2](nationalinstruments-veristand-clientapi-ialarmmanager2.html) interface if you want to specify one of multiple targets.

This method is deprecated in NI VeriStand 2010 and later.

#### Parameters

| Name | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| alarmNames | string[] | Specifies the names of the alarms for which you want to get information. |
| timeout | uint | Specifies the time, in milliseconds, for this method to attempt to read data from the alarm manager before returning an error. |
| alarmInfo | out AlarmInfo[] | Returns the alarm information. Use this parameter with the properties of the AlarmInfo class to get specific information about an alarm, such as its high limit, low limit, mode, priority, and state. |

#### Returns

Returns an NationalInstruments.VeriStand.Error object. If no error occurs, the Code property of the Error object is 0.

Parent topic:

Use the GetMultipleAlarmsData method of the IAlarmManager2 interface instead, which allows you to get specific information about an alarm, such as its status. |
| GetMultipleAlarmsData(string[], uint, out AlarmInfo[]) | This method from the IAlarmManager interface gets a list of all the alarms running on the first target. However, National Instruments recommends that you use the GetMultipleAlarmsData method of the IAlarmManager2 interface instead of this deprecated method. |

Parent topic:

## TOPIC 00147: GetAlarmsStatus(string, out bool, out bool, out bool, out string, out string, out string)

- bundle_id: `veristand-net-api-ref`
- source_path: `nationalinstruments-veristand-clientapi-ialarmmanager2-getalarmsstatus__string-out-out-out-out-out-out.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/veristand-net-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/nationalinstruments-veristand-clientapi-ialarmmanager2-getalarmsstatus__string-out-out-out-out-out-out.html
- document_id: `veristand-net-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: This method is obsolete in NI VeriStand 2011 and later. Use the GetMultipleAlarmsData method instead, which allows you to get specific information about an alarm, such as its status. SyntaxNamespace: NationalInstruments.VeriStand.ClientAPIpublic Error GetAlarmsStatus(string target, out bool highAlar

### GetAlarmsStatus(string, out bool, out bool, out bool, out string, out string, out string)

This method is obsolete in NI VeriStand 2011 and later. Use the [GetMultipleAlarmsData](nationalinstruments-veristand-clientapi-ialarmmanager2-getmultiplealarmsdata__string-string_arr1-uint-out.html) method instead, which allows you to get specific information about an alarm, such as its status.

#### Syntax

**Namespace:**[NationalInstruments.VeriStand.ClientAPI](nationalinstruments-veristand-clientapi.html)

public [Error](nationalinstruments-veristand-clientapi-stimulusresult.html) GetAlarmsStatus(string target, out bool highAlarm, out bool medAlarm, out bool lowAlarm, out string highAlarmName, out string medAlarmName, out string lowAlarmName)

#### Remarks

Gets the status of the high, medium, and low-priority alarms running on the first target. However, strict priorities of low, medium, and high are no longer supported. Valid priorities now range from 0 - 31. This method only tests alarms in group 0.

#### Parameters

| Name | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| target | string | Specifies the name of the target to query. |
| highAlarm | out bool | Returns TRUE if a high-priority alarm is triggered. |
| medAlarm | out bool | Returns TRUE if a medium-priority alarm is triggered. |
| lowAlarm | out bool | Returns TRUE if a low-priority alarm is triggered. |
| highAlarmName | out string | Returns the name of the currently active, high-priority alarm. |
| medAlarmName | out string | Returns the name of the currently active, medium-priority alarm. |
| lowAlarmName | out string | Returns the name of the currently active, low-priority alarm. |

#### Returns

Returns an NationalInstruments.VeriStand.Error object. If no error occurs, the Code property of the Error object is 0.

Parent topic:

IAlarmManager2 Interface

### IAlarmManager2 Interface

Interface to control and observe alarms running on a target. Use the [GetIAlarmManager2](nationalinstruments-veristand-clientapi-factory-getialarmmanager2__string.html) method of the [Factory](nationalinstruments-veristand-clientapi-factory.html) class to access this interface.

#### Derives from

- IAlarmManager

#### Syntax

**Namespace:**[NationalInstruments.VeriStand.ClientAPI](nationalinstruments-veristand-clientapi.html)

public interface IAlarmManager2 : IAlarmManager

#### Remarks

This interface also inherits the methods of the [IAlarmManager](nationalinstruments-veristand-clientapi-ialarmmanager.html) interface.

#### Methods

| Name | Description |
| --- | --- |
| GetAlarmList(string, out string[]) | Gets a list of all the alarms running on the target. |
| GetAlarmsStatus(string, out bool, out bool, out bool, out string, out string, out string) | This method is obsolete in NI VeriStand 2011 and later. Use the GetMultipleAlarmsData method instead, which allows you to get specific information about an alarm, such as its status. |
| GetMultipleAlarmsData(string, string[], uint, out AlarmInfo[]) | Gets information for multiple alarms running on the specified target. |
| RegisterForAlarmChange(string, string, EventHandler< AlarmChangeEventArgs >) | Registers a delegate for a change in a particular alarm. |
| SetAlarmsAcknowledgementStatus(string, string[], AcknowledgementStatus) | Sets the acknowledgement status of alarms running on the specified target. |

#### Events

| Name | Description |
| --- | --- |

| OnAlarmTrigger2 | Callback invoked when an alarm is triggered. |

- bundle_id: `veristand-net-api-ref`
- source_path: `nationalinstruments-veristand-clientapi-icalibration-getcalibration__string-out-out-out-out-out-out-out-out.html`

- document_id: `veristand-net-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Reads the current calibration settings for a channel. SyntaxNamespace: NationalInstruments.VeriStand.ClientAPIpublic Error GetCalibration(string channelName, out ScaleType scaleType, out double[] coefficients, out ThermocoupleType thermocoupleType, out TemperatureUnits units, out CJCType cjcType, ou

### GetCalibration(string, out ScaleType, out double[], out ThermocoupleType, out TemperatureUnits, out CJCType, out string, out double, out double)

Reads the current calibration settings for a channel.

#### Syntax

**Namespace:**[NationalInstruments.VeriStand.ClientAPI](nationalinstruments-veristand-clientapi.html)

public [Error](nationalinstruments-veristand-clientapi-stimulusresult.html) GetCalibration(string channelName, out ScaleType scaleType, out double[] coefficients, out ThermocoupleType thermocoupleType, out TemperatureUnits units, out CJCType cjcType, out string cjcChannelName, out double offset, out double scale)

#### Parameters

| Name | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| channelName | string | The name of the channel from which to get calibration information. |
| scaleType | out ScaleType | The ScaleType of the calibration scale. |
| coefficients | out double[] | The coefficients of the polynomial scale. (Valid only if ScaleType is 0 — Polynomial.) |
| thermocoupleType | out ThermocoupleType | The ThermocoupleType. (Valid only if ScaleType is 1 — Thermocouple.) |
| units | out TemperatureUnits | The TemperatureUnits of the calibrated value. (Valid only if ScaleType is 1 — Thermocouple.) |
| cjcType | out CJCType | The CJCType of the cold junction compensation sensor. (Valid only if ScaleType is 1 — Thermocouple.) |
| cjcChannelName | out string | The name of the cold junction compensation channel. (Valid only if ScaleType is 1 — Thermocouple.) |
| offset | out double | The offset applied after primary scaling. |
| scale | out double | The scale applied after primary scaling. |

#### Returns

Returns an error if the calibration component is not available or if the channel is not scalable. If no error occurs, the Code property of the Error object is 0.

Parent topic:

ICalibration Interface

- source_description: Sets calibration for a channel using a polynomial scale. You also can use the SetThermocoupleCalibration method to set calibration using a thermocouple scale. A single channel can have only one scale. SyntaxNamespace: NationalInstruments.VeriStand.ClientAPIpublic Error SetPolynomialCalibration(strin

### SetPolynomialCalibration(string, double[], double, double)

Sets calibration for a channel using a polynomial scale. You also can use the [SetThermocoupleCalibration](nationalinstruments-veristand-clientapi-icalibration-setthermocouplecalibration__string-thermocoupletype-temperatureunits-cjctype-string-double-double.html) method to set calibration using a thermocouple scale. A single channel can have only one scale.

#### Syntax

**Namespace:**[NationalInstruments.VeriStand.ClientAPI](nationalinstruments-veristand-clientapi.html)

public [Error](nationalinstruments-veristand-clientapi-stimulusresult.html) SetPolynomialCalibration(string channelName, double[] coefficients, double offset, double scale)

#### Remarks

*y* = *c*[0] + *c*[1] * *x* + *c*[2] * *x*^2 + *c*[3] * *x*^3

#### Parameters

| Name | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| channelName | string | The name of channel on which to set calibration. |
| coefficients | double[] | The coefficients of the polynomial scale. You can specify up to four coefficients. |

#### Parameters

| Name | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| offset | double | The offset to apply after primary scaling. |
| scale | double | The scale to apply after the primary scaling. |

#### Returns

Returns an error if the calibration component is not available or if the channel is not scalable. If no error occurs, the Code property of the Error object is 0.

Sets calibration for a channel using a thermocouple scale where the raw voltage is converted to a temperature. | thermocoupleType | ThermocoupleType | The ThermocoupleType. |
| units | TemperatureUnits | The TemperatureUnits of the calibrated value. |
| cjcType | CJCType | The CJCType of the cold junction compensation sensor. |

## TOPIC 00161: ICalibration Interface

- bundle_id: `veristand-net-api-ref`
- source_path: `nationalinstruments-veristand-clientapi-icalibration.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/veristand-net-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/nationalinstruments-veristand-clientapi-icalibration.html
- document_id: `veristand-net-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: This interface is obsolete in NI VeriStand 2012 and later. Use the ICalibration2 interface instead. Interface to get and set calibration settings for channels on the test system. Use the GetICalibration method of the Factory class to access this interface. This interface is associated with the legac

### ICalibration Interface

This interface is obsolete in NI VeriStand 2012 and later. Use the [ICalibration2](nationalinstruments-veristand-clientapi-icalibration2.html) interface instead. Interface to get and set calibration settings for channels on the test system. Use the [GetICalibration](nationalinstruments-veristand-clientapi-factory-geticalibration__string.html) method of the [Factory](nationalinstruments-veristand-clientapi-factory.html) class to access this interface. This interface is associated with the legacy calibration feature.

#### Derives from

None

#### Syntax

**Namespace:**[NationalInstruments.VeriStand.ClientAPI](nationalinstruments-veristand-clientapi.html)

public interface ICalibration

#### Methods

| Name | Description |
| --- | --- |
| GetCalibration(string, out ScaleType, out double[], out ThermocoupleType, out TemperatureUnits, out CJCType, out string, out double, out double) | Reads the current calibration settings for a channel. |
| GetRawValue(string, out double) | Gets the raw value reading for a calibrated channel. For input channels, the raw value is the value read from the device. For output channels, the raw value is the value written to the device. |
| GetRawValues(string[], out double[]) | Gets the raw value readings for a list of calibrated channels. For input channels, the raw value is the value read from the device. For output channels, the raw value is the value written to the device. |
| RemoveCalibration(string) | Removes any calibration that was previously set for a channel. |
| SetPolynomialCalibration(string, double[], double, double) | Sets calibration for a channel using a polynomial scale. You also can use the SetThermocoupleCalibration method to set calibration using a thermocouple scale. A single channel can have only one scale. |
| SetThermocoupleCalibration(string, ThermocoupleType, TemperatureUnits, CJCType, string, double, double) | Sets calibration for a channel using a thermocouple scale where the raw voltage is converted to a temperature. You also can use the SetPolynomialCalibration method to set calibration using a polynomial scale. A single channel can have only one scale. |

Parent topic:

NationalInstruments.VeriStand.ClientAPI

## TOPIC 00181: SendMessage(string, byte[], uint, out byte[])

- bundle_id: `veristand-net-api-ref`
- source_path: `nationalinstruments-veristand-clientapi-icustomdevice-sendmessage__string-byte_arr1-uint-out.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/veristand-net-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/nationalinstruments-veristand-clientapi-icustomdevice-sendmessage__string-byte_arr1-uint-out.html
- document_id: `veristand-net-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Sends a message or command to a custom device in an NI VeriStand project, as well as data required by the case that handles the command. You can use this method with any custom device that registers to receive the command you specify. SyntaxNamespace: NationalInstruments.VeriStand.ClientAPIpublic Er

### SendMessage(string, byte[], uint, out byte[])

Sends a message or command to a custom device in an NI VeriStand project, as well as data required by the case that handles the command. You can use this method with any custom device that registers to receive the *command*  you specify.

#### Syntax

**Namespace:**[NationalInstruments.VeriStand.ClientAPI](nationalinstruments-veristand-clientapi.html)

public [Error](nationalinstruments-veristand-clientapi-stimulusresult.html) SendMessage(string command, byte[] data, uint timeout, out byte[] response)

#### Remarks

This method sends data as a byte array of 8-bit unsigned integer values. You also can use the NationalInstruments.VeriStand.ClientAPI.ICustomDevice.SendMessage(string, byte[], uint, out byte[]) method to send data as a string of human-readable characters.

#### Parameters

| Name | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| command | string | The message or command to send to the custom device. |
| data | byte[] | Data to send to the custom device. |
| timeout | uint | Time in milliseconds to wait for a response from the custom device before returning an error. |
| response | out byte[] | Returns the response from the custom device to the command . |

#### Returns

Returns an NationalInstruments.VeriStand.Error object. If no error occurs, the Code property of the Error object is 0.

Parent topic:

ICustomDevice Interface

<!--NI_TOPIC bundle=veristand-net-api-ref path=nationalinstruments-veristand-clientapi-icustomdevice-sendmessage__string-string-uint-out.html language=enus -->
## TOPIC 00182: SendMessage(string, string, uint, out string)

- bundle_id: `veristand-net-api-ref`
- source_path: `nationalinstruments-veristand-clientapi-icustomdevice-sendmessage__string-string-uint-out.html`

- document_id: `veristand-net-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Sends a message or command to a custom device in an NI VeriStand project, as well as data required by the case that handles the command. You can use this method with any custom device that registers to receive the command you specify. SyntaxNamespace: NationalInstruments.VeriStand.ClientAPIpublic Er

### SendMessage(string, string, uint, out string)

Sends a message or command to a custom device in an NI VeriStand project, as well as data required by the case that handles the command. You can use this method with any custom device that registers to receive the *command*  you specify.

#### Syntax

**Namespace:**[NationalInstruments.VeriStand.ClientAPI](nationalinstruments-veristand-clientapi.html)

public [Error](nationalinstruments-veristand-clientapi-stimulusresult.html) SendMessage(string command, string data, uint timeout, out string response)

#### Remarks

This method sends string data to a custom device. You also can use the NationalInstruments.VeriStand.ClientAPI.ICustomDevice.SendMessage(string, byte[], uint, out byte[]) method to send data as a byte array of 8-bit unsigned integer values.

#### Parameters

| Name | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| command | string | The message or command to send to the custom device. |
| data | string | Data to send to the custom device. This input expects only human-readable string characters. If you send other string characters, such as a null character, this method might truncate the message during transmission to the custom device. If the data you want to send contains null characters, convert the string to a byte array and use the NationalInstruments.VeriStand.ClientAPI.ICustomDevice.SendMessage(string, byte[], uint, out byte[]) method to send the data to the custom device. |
| timeout | uint | Time in milliseconds to wait for a response from the custom device before returning an error. |
| response | out string | Returns the response from the custom device to the command . |

#### Returns

Returns an NationalInstruments.VeriStand.Error object. If no error occurs, the Code property of the Error object is 0.

Parent topic:

Returns an NationalInstruments.VeriStand.Error object. If no error occurs, the Code property of the Error object is 0.

### StopPlaying()

Stops the Macro Player. This method returns the Macro Player to the idle state and resets the macro you are playing back to the beginning of the recording. If you want to be able to resume playback from the place where you stop it, use the [PausePlaying](nationalinstruments-veristand-clientapi-imacroplayer-pauseplaying.html) method instead.

#### Syntax

**Namespace:**[NationalInstruments.VeriStand.ClientAPI](nationalinstruments-veristand-clientapi.html)

## TOPIC 00208: IMacroPlayer Interface

- bundle_id: `veristand-net-api-ref`
- source_path: `nationalinstruments-veristand-clientapi-imacroplayer.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/veristand-net-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/nationalinstruments-veristand-clientapi-imacroplayer.html
- document_id: `veristand-net-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Interface to the Macro Player tool. Use this interface to load and play back a macro (.nivsmacro) file you created using the IMacroRecorder interface. Use the GetIMacroPlayer method of the Factory class to access this interface. Derives fromNoneSyntaxNamespace: NationalInstruments.VeriStand.ClientAP

### IMacroPlayer Interface

Interface to the Macro Player tool. Use this interface to load and play back a macro (.nivsmacro) file you created using the [IMacroRecorder](nationalinstruments-veristand-clientapi-imacrorecorder.html) interface. Use the [GetIMacroPlayer](nationalinstruments-veristand-clientapi-factory-getimacroplayer__string.html) method of the [Factory](nationalinstruments-veristand-clientapi-factory.html) class to access this interface.

#### Derives from

None

#### Syntax

**Namespace:**[NationalInstruments.VeriStand.ClientAPI](nationalinstruments-veristand-clientapi.html)

public interface IMacroPlayer

#### Methods

| Name | Description |
| --- | --- |
| GetCommandLines(out WorkspaceMacro.CommandLineInfo[]) | Gets the currently loaded command lines. You can use the members of the CommandLineInfo class of the NationalInstruments.VeriStand.WorkspaceMacro assembly to get information about the command lines this method returns. |
| LoadMacro(string) | Loads a previously recorded macro (.nivsmacro) file for playback. |
| PausePlaying() | Pauses the playback of a macro file. |
| PlayMacro(PlayModeEnum) | Runs the Macro Player tool and specifies the speed at which to play back macro files. |
| PlayState() | Gets the current state of the Macro Player tool. |
| ResumePlaying() | Resumes the playback of a macro file. This method plays back the file from the point at which the PausePlaying method paused playback. |
| StopPlaying() | Stops the Macro Player. This method returns the Macro Player to the idle state and resets the macro you are playing back to the beginning of the recording. If you want to be able to resume playback from the place where you stop it, use the PausePlaying method instead. |
| Wait() | Waits for the Macro Player tool to finish playing back the current macro file before returning and continuing execution. |

#### Events

| Name | Description |
| --- | --- |
| OnMacroCommandLine | Callback invoked just before executing a Macro Player command. |
| OnMacroComplete | Callback invoked when the Macro Player completes execution. |
| OnMacroErrorMessage | Callback invoked if an error occurs while attempting to execute a Macro Player command. |
| OnMacroPercentComplete | Callback invoked after executing a Macro Player command. The percent is calculated using the length of time a command takes to execute relative to the total time required for all commands to execute. |

Parent topic:

NationalInstruments.VeriStand.ClientAPI

### SaveMacro(string)

Saves the current macro recording. You must use the [StopRecording](nationalinstruments-veristand-clientapi-imacrorecorder-stoprecording.html) method to stop recording before you call this method. This method creates a file of the type .nivsmacro. You can use the [IMacroPlayer](nationalinstruments-veristand-clientapi-imacroplayer.html) interface to load the file this method creates and to play back the saved recording.

#### Returns

This method Returns an NationalInstruments.VeriStand.Error object. If no error occurs the Code property of the Error object is 0. If the Macro Recorder is still in record mode, the Code property is 1. If another error occurs, the Code property is 2.

## TOPIC 00215: IMacroRecorder Interface

- bundle_id: `veristand-net-api-ref`
- source_path: `nationalinstruments-veristand-clientapi-imacrorecorder.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/veristand-net-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/nationalinstruments-veristand-clientapi-imacrorecorder.html
- document_id: `veristand-net-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Interface to the Macro Recorder tool. You can use the members of this interface to record commands the VeriStand Gateway sends to a target. You can save the recorded commands to a macro (.nivsmacro) file to later play back using the IMacroPlayer interface. Use the GetIMacroRecorder method of the Fac

### IMacroRecorder Interface

Interface to the Macro Recorder tool. You can use the members of this interface to record commands the VeriStand Gateway sends to a target. You can save the recorded commands to a macro (.nivsmacro) file to later play back using the [IMacroPlayer](nationalinstruments-veristand-clientapi-imacroplayer.html) interface. Use the [GetIMacroRecorder](nationalinstruments-veristand-clientapi-factory-getimacrorecorder.html) method of the [Factory](nationalinstruments-veristand-clientapi-factory.html) class to access this interface.

#### Derives from

None

#### Syntax

**Namespace:**[NationalInstruments.VeriStand.ClientAPI](nationalinstruments-veristand-clientapi.html)

public interface IMacroRecorder

#### Methods

| Name | Description |
| --- | --- |
| GetCommandLines(out WorkspaceMacro.CommandLineInfo[]) | Gets the currently loaded command lines. You can use the members of the CommandLineInfo class of the NationalInstruments.VeriStand.WorkspaceMacro assembly to get information about the command lines this method returns. |
| ResumeRecording() | Resumes a stopped macro recording. Use this method after the StopRecording method to append information to the existing macro (.nivsmacro) file in memory. |
| SaveMacro(string) | Saves the current macro recording. You must use the StopRecording method to stop recording before you call this method. This method creates a file of the type .nivsmacro. You can use the IMacroPlayer interface to load the file this method creates and to play back the saved recording. |
| StartRecording() | Starts a new macro recording. If an unsaved macro file is in memory, this method removes that file from memory and creates a new file when recording begins. |
| StopRecording() | Stops the current macro recording. This method does not save the recording or remove the recording from memory. Use the SaveMacro method to save the current recording. Use the ResumeRecording method to resume the current recording. |

#### Events

| Name | Description |
| --- | --- |
| OnMacroCommandLine | Callback invoked just before a command to the Macro Recorder is logged. |

Parent topic:

NationalInstruments.VeriStand.ClientAPI

<!--NI_TOPIC bundle=veristand-net-api-ref path=nationalinstruments-veristand-clientapi-imodel-getmodelexecutionstate__out-out.html language=enus -->

### SetModelExecutionState(ModelCommand)

Sets the current execution state of a model.

Note

This method initiates a request operation on the server. Successful invocation of the method does not imply that the state of the model has changed.

#### Syntax

**Namespace:**[NationalInstruments.VeriStand.ClientAPI](nationalinstruments-veristand-clientapi.html)

public [Error](nationalinstruments-veristand-clientapi-stimulusresult.html) SetModelExecutionState(ModelCommand command)

#### Parameters

| Name | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| command | ModelCommand | The ModelCommand, or execution state. |

#### Returns

This method returns an error if no configuration is running on the workspace. If no error occurs, the Code property of the Error object is 0.

Parent topic:

IModel Interface

### IModel Interface

Interface to control and observe a specific model running on the execution host. Use the [GetIModel(string)](nationalinstruments-veristand-clientapi-factory-getimodel__string.html) method of the [Factory](nationalinstruments-veristand-clientapi-factory.html) class to access this interface.

public interface IModel

#### Methods

| Name | Description |
| --- | --- |
| GetModelExecutionState(out double, out ModelState) | Gets the state and running time of a model. |
| RestoreModelState(string) | Restores a model to the state defined by the file you specify. |
| SaveModelState(string) | Saves data about the current state of a model running on the target to an XML file that you specify. |
| SetModelExecutionState(ModelCommand) | Sets the current execution state of a model. Note This method initiates a request operation on the server. Successful invocation of the method does not imply that the state of the model has changed. |

## TOPIC 00246: UpdateParametersFromFile(string, string[])

- bundle_id: `veristand-net-api-ref`
- source_path: `nationalinstruments-veristand-clientapi-imodelmanager2-updateparametersfromfile__string-string_arr1.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/veristand-net-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/nationalinstruments-veristand-clientapi-imodelmanager2-updateparametersfromfile__string-string_arr1.html
- document_id: `veristand-net-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Updates a set of model parameters using parameter values stored in a set of files. SyntaxNamespace: NationalInstruments.VeriStand.ClientAPIpublic Error UpdateParametersFromFile(string target, string[] parameter_files)ParametersNameTypeDescriptiontargetstringThe name of the target to query. This para

### UpdateParametersFromFile(string, string[])

Updates a set of model parameters using parameter values stored in a set of files.

#### Syntax

**Namespace:**[NationalInstruments.VeriStand.ClientAPI](nationalinstruments-veristand-clientapi.html)

public [Error](nationalinstruments-veristand-clientapi-stimulusresult.html) UpdateParametersFromFile(string target, string[] parameter_files)

#### Parameters

| Name | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| target | string | The name of the target to query. This parameter expects the name of the target as specified in the system definition file. For example: Controller |
| parameter_files | string[] | The paths to the files that contain the new parameter values. |

#### Returns

Returns an NationalInstruments.VeriStand.Error object. This method returns ComponentNotAvailable if the current configuration does not support parameter configuration. If no error occurs, the Code property of the Error object is 0.

Parent topic:

IModelManager2 Interface

## TOPIC 00247: IModelManager2 Interface

- bundle_id: `veristand-net-api-ref`
- source_path: `nationalinstruments-veristand-clientapi-imodelmanager2.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/veristand-net-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/nationalinstruments-veristand-clientapi-imodelmanager2.html
- document_id: `veristand-net-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Interface to control and observe models running on an execution host. Use the GetIModelManager2 method of the Factory class to access this interface. Derives fromIModelManagerSyntaxNamespace: NationalInstruments.VeriStand.ClientAPIpublic interface IModelManager2 : IModelManagerRemarksThis interface

### IModelManager2 Interface

Interface to control and observe models running on an execution host. Use the [GetIModelManager2](nationalinstruments-veristand-clientapi-factory-getimodelmanager2__string.html) method of the [Factory](nationalinstruments-veristand-clientapi-factory.html) class to access this interface.

#### Derives from

- IModelManager

#### Syntax

**Namespace:**[NationalInstruments.VeriStand.ClientAPI](nationalinstruments-veristand-clientapi.html)

public interface IModelManager2 : IModelManager

#### Remarks

This interface also inherits the methods of the [IModelManager](nationalinstruments-veristand-clientapi-imodelmanager.html) interface.

#### Methods

| Name | Description |
| --- | --- |
| GetModelList(string, out string[]) | Gets a list of all the models running on the specified target. |
| GetMultipleParameterDataArrayValues(string, string[], out DataArray[]) | Gets the values of multiple model parameters present on the specified target. |
| GetMultipleParameterValues(string, string[], out double[]) | Gets the values of multiple model parameters present on the specified target. |
| GetParametersList(string, out string[]) | Gets a list of all the model parameters present on the specified target. |
| GetParametersList(string, out string[], out uint[], out uint[]) | Gets a list of all the model parameters present on the specified target. |
| GetParameterVectorValues(string, string, out uint, out uint, out double[]) | Gets a two-dimensional vector array of values for a single model parameter present on the specified target. |
| GetSignalValues(string, string, int[], int, out double[]) | Reads values for the specified scalar model signals. |
| GetSignalValues(string, string, int[], out double[]) | Reads values for the specified scalar model signals with an infinite timeout. |
| GetSingleParameterValue(string, string, out double) | Gets the value of a single model parameter present on the specified target. |
| RegisterForParameterValueChange(string, string, EventHandler< ParameterValueChangeEventArgs >) | Registers a delegate for a change in a particular model parameter. |
| SetMultipleParameterValues(string, string[], double[]) | Sets the values of multiple model parameters present on the specified target. |
| SetParameterValues(string, string[], DataArray[]) | Sets the values of multiple model parameters present on the specified execution host. |
| SetParameterVectorValues(string, string, double[]) | Sets a two-dimensional vector array of values for a single model parameter present on the specified target. |
| SetSingleParameterValue(string, string, double) | Sets the value of a single model parameter present on the specified target. |
| UnregisterForParameterValueChange(string, string, EventHandler< ParameterValueChangeEventArgs >) | Unregisters a delegate for a change in a particular model parameter. |
| UpdateParametersFromFile(string, string[]) | Updates a set of model parameters using parameter values stored in a set of files. |

#### Events

| Name | Description |
| --- | --- |
| ParameterValueChanged | Allows users to subscribe/unsubscribe directly to the global parameter change event. Any parameter change will raise this event to notify those registered. |

Parent topic:

NationalInstruments.VeriStand.ClientAPI

## TOPIC 00250: Connect()

- bundle_id: `veristand-net-api-ref`
- source_path: `nationalinstruments-veristand-clientapi-iproject-connect.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/veristand-net-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/nationalinstruments-veristand-clientapi-iproject-connect.html
- document_id: `veristand-net-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Connects an NI VeriStand project on the host computer to the target. This method only establishes a connection to a target. It does not deploy the system definition file. Use Deploy() to deploy a system definition file to the target. SyntaxNamespace: NationalInstruments.VeriStand.ClientAPIpublic Err

### Connect()

Connects an NI VeriStand project on the host computer to the target. This method only establishes a connection to a target. It does not deploy the system definition file. Use [Deploy()](nationalinstruments-veristand-clientapi-iproject-deploy.html) to deploy a system definition file to the target.

#### Syntax

**Namespace:**[NationalInstruments.VeriStand.ClientAPI](nationalinstruments-veristand-clientapi.html)

public [Error](nationalinstruments-veristand-clientapi-stimulusresult.html) Connect()

#### Returns

Returns an NationalInstruments.VeriStand.Error object. If no error occurs, the Code property of the Error object is 0.

Parent topic:

IProject Interface
